<div id="review_152059911" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/152059911" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/152059911?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-lara-adrian">author-lara-adrian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=the-hymen-club">the-hymen-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=signed-by-author">signed-by-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer152059911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8970590432144926949">With the way Lara Adrian ended the last book, Deeper than Midnight, I was dying to get my hands on this one. This is Sterling Chase’s book, the former Agency member, the one who was straight arrow before his life made a turn for the worse.<br/><br/>Chase has endured a lot. He has lost many things in his life – the loss of his brother, Quinton, the loss of the woman he loved, Elise to another Breed member, the loss of his nephew, Camden and now, the imminent loss of his sanity, which will also mean the los</span>
  <span id="freeText8970590432144926949" style="display:none">With the way Lara Adrian ended the last book, Deeper than Midnight, I was dying to get my hands on this one. This is Sterling Chase’s book, the former Agency member, the one who was straight arrow before his life made a turn for the worse.<br /><br />Chase has endured a lot. He has lost many things in his life – the loss of his brother, Quinton, the loss of the woman he loved, Elise to another Breed member, the loss of his nephew, Camden and now, the imminent loss of his sanity, which will also mean the loss of his place amongst the warriors of the Order.<br /><br />When Chase gives himself up to the uniforms in the last book, my head was reeling. I will admit, there were times in the past where Chase made the wrong decisions that impacted the Order greatly. He was becoming a liability more than an asset to them, but giving himself up so that the Order could gain some more time was his final act to show the others, and maybe himself, that he wasn’t completely lost to Bloodlust.<br /><br />I was eager to know more about Tavia Fairchild. However, her secrets about her past caught me by surprise. Though she isn’t my favourite Breedmate (that honor goes to Renata and Tess), I found that I admired her courage and strength throughout the book. I say this often about Adrian’s heroines. She always writes strong women who actively take part in the conflict of the stories and I love that, who wouldn’t?<br /><br />Chase and Tavia’s attraction for one another is instant, though they try to fight it. What tired me was the fact that Chase still held himself back, believing himself to be unworthy for her love. He didn’t want to be the staining mark on her life that she’d remember long after he was gone. And he would be, that’s just who Chase is. He believed himself to be unreliable and dangerous and creating a blood bond between them would be a big mistake.<br /><br />Once I got over that initial frustration, I was able to get into the book more. Adrian answers some questions readers have been asking for awhile, such as how did the Breedmates come to be. And finally, the war with Dragos comes to an end.<br /><br />I’ve always thought that Adrian wrote great actions scenes, but the war between the Order and Dragos didn’t really live up to her usual standards. It was good, but not the explosive war I thought it would be.<br /><br />I’m hoping this isn’t the last of the Midnight Breed books. As long as she keeps writing them, I’ll continue to read them. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8970590432144926949" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_285210457" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/285210457" />
    <a title="Diana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3373844-diana"><img alt="Diana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489004797p2/3373844.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/285210457?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Diana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Diana" href="/user/show/3373844-diana">Diana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3373844-diana?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3373844-diana?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3373844-diana?shelf=soa-review">soa-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer285210457" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3061088774787036684">Audiobook Narrated by Hillary Huber<br/><br/>I’ve listened to seven of the books in the Midnight Breed series so I was interested in catching up with Darker After Midnight, the tenth book that was billed as the wrapup. I recommend the first four in the series which have intricate plots and real romance. As to this latest book, it’s no spoiler to reveal that the Order’s super evil archenemy Dragos is finally vanquished, albeit fairly easily, after nine books of buildup. Apparently the publisher had second </span>
  <span id="freeText3061088774787036684" style="display:none">Audiobook Narrated by Hillary Huber<br /><br />I’ve listened to seven of the books in the Midnight Breed series so I was interested in catching up with Darker After Midnight, the tenth book that was billed as the wrapup. I recommend the first four in the series which have intricate plots and real romance. As to this latest book, it’s no spoiler to reveal that the Order’s super evil archenemy Dragos is finally vanquished, albeit fairly easily, after nine books of buildup. Apparently the publisher had second thoughts and there now will be at least three more which explains the heavy presence of the younger generation in this book. In fact it seems that every character who ever set foot in one of the Midnight Breed books has a featured role, leaving the main couple Tavia and Chase competing for air time with a boatload of previous couples sappy with baby fever.<br /><br />Normally I would issue a warning not to start a series with book #10 but I think you could with this one. Author Adrian painstakingly explains the series mythology and you get to meet the whole Breed gang. The commercial tone is hard to miss.<br /><br />There is one obvious and significant difference between Adrian’s Midnight Breed series and its inspiration, the Black Dagger Brotherhood series by J.R. Ward. Ward’s vampires get it that they’re high camp with a wink wink, nudge nudge. Adrian’s supernaturals take themselves very, very seriously making them too deadly and humorless for me. A surprise Extremely Important Event for the Breed Nation occurs in the epilogue. I laughed out loud, in a room by myself, in the dark, and I’m pretty sure I wasn’t supposed to find it funny.<br /><br />Narrator Hillary Huber has done a fine job with all of this series. She’s handled a number of accents with aplomb. So many characters from the previous books appeared here that I had some difficulty knowing who was speaking at times but Huber kept a handle on it. My only complaint is with the child Mira sounding too babyish, but she’ll probably be grown and ready for her very own fated mate in the next entry to the series.<br /><br />See my audiobook reviews at Blue Moon<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://saschakeet.wordpress.com/">http://saschakeet.wordpress.com/</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3061088774787036684" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1411570652722614877">I have been waiting for Stirling Chase's story for a long time and finally, it's here.<br/><br/>What a great 'FINALE" to the Midnight Breed Series.....so much happens in this story that just blows your mind. <br/><br/>Fast-paced, a riveting and dark world filled with characters that stay with you for a long time.<br/><br/>Firstly, I loved Chase and Tavia Fairchild.   <span id="freeText1411570652722614877" style="display:none">I have been waiting for Stirling Chase's story for a long time and finally, it's here.<br /><br />What a great 'FINALE" to the Midnight Breed Series.....so much happens in this story that just blows your mind. <br /><br />Fast-paced, a riveting and dark world filled with characters that stay with you for a long time.<br /><br />Firstly, I loved Chase and Tavia Fairchild. A dark, tortured hero and a heroine that I never expected....don't want to spoil what it was.....you find out!!! Their chemistry, both sexual and emotional was beyond amazing!!!!!<br /><br />A final show-down between the Breed warriors and their mates and the evil Dragos. <br /><br />Chaos reigns in planet Earth with some really unexpected surprises.<br /><br />This is such a fabulous series and if you love vampires with a "difference", then read every book.<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8346689762113805411">The end of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12042279.Darker_After_Midnight__Midnight_Breed___10_' title='Darker After Midnight (Midnight Breed, #10) by Lara Adrian' rel='nofollow noopener'>Darker After Midnight</a> feels as though it was intended to be the end of the Midnight Breed series. That’s what I thought when I read this several years back. There are four more books to the series, the last of which I haven’t yet read, which is why I am rereading the others. The action-packed plot and the romance between Tavia and Chase make this one of my favorites.</span>
  <span id="freeText8346689762113805411" style="display:none">The end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12042279.Darker_After_Midnight__Midnight_Breed___10_" title="Darker After Midnight (Midnight Breed, #10) by Lara Adrian" rel="nofollow noopener">Darker After Midnight</a> feels as though it was intended to be the end of the Midnight Breed series. That’s what I thought when I read this several years back. There are four more books to the series, the last of which I haven’t yet read, which is why I am rereading the others. The action-packed plot and the romance between Tavia and Chase make this one of my favorites.</span>

<div id="review_179764674" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/179764674" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/179764674?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/13486075-darker-after-midnight">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=for-review-read">for-review-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=2019-love-letters-berlin">2019-love-letters-berlin</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer179764674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10147027268220914571">It's no secret that I'm a massive fan of the Midnight Breed series, in fact I'm happy to say it's my favourite adult paranormal romance series! I'm always desperate to get my hands on the next installment and because I'm such a big fan I always have high expectations. Lara Adrian hasn't let me down yet and she always manages to make each book better than the last. Darker After Midnight is no exception and I can't begin to tell you how awesome this book actually is, in fact I'm still struggling t</span>
  <span id="freeText10147027268220914571" style="display:none">It's no secret that I'm a massive fan of the Midnight Breed series, in fact I'm happy to say it's my favourite adult paranormal romance series! I'm always desperate to get my hands on the next installment and because I'm such a big fan I always have high expectations. Lara Adrian hasn't let me down yet and she always manages to make each book better than the last. Darker After Midnight is no exception and I can't begin to tell you how awesome this book actually is, in fact I'm still struggling to put into words just how much I loved it. Although this review won't contain spoilers for Darker After Midnight please note that this is book 10 in the series and it is impossible to write a review without mentioning events from previous books so you may not want to read further if you're not up to date with the series. If you're new to the series then I can't recommend it highly enough, although each book can probably be read as a stand alone I would highly recommend reading them in order starting with Kiss of Midnight.<br /><br />The story picks up immediately after the ending of Deeper than Midnight, Chase has given himself up to the human police to allow the rest of the Warriors to escape from the compound with their mates. He is on the verge of blood lust but is trying to redeem himself after the trouble he has caused for his friends recently. Tavia is working for a senator who has just become Dragos' latest minion, she was a witness to Chase's attempt at assassinating Dragos and their paths cross again when she comes to the police station to identify him. It doesn't take long for Chase to discover that Tavia is not all that she seems and he quickly realises just how important she is for the future of the breed. Dragos is after Tavia but that is the least of their problems as he has much bigger plans, plans that will cause complete chaos for all of the breed. Can Chase and the Warriors stop him in time?<br /><br />I think I'm in the minority when I say I wasn't a massive fan of Chase, it wasn't that I didn't like him - he just wasn't my favourite Breed male. It wasn't until towards the end of Deeper than Midnight that I really started to get excited about reading his story but I really loved him by the end of his book. For someone who was such a stickler for the rules Chase fell a long way as he came closer and closer to giving into his blood lust. He knows he has let down his friends at the compound and is scared to act on his feelings for Tavia in case he ends up hurting her. He is embarrassed by his actions in the past and wants to be able to earn back the trust of Lucan and the others but doesn't really know where to start. Tavia really surprised me, I had suspicions about her before the big reveal but really didn't have a clue what was to come. It shocked the heck out of me but I mean that in a good way! She was a great heroine and although she was wary of Chase and the other warriors she stood up for herself and didn't sit back and wait to be looked after.<br /><br />There are so many things going on in Darker After Midnight that I really couldn't put it down. Alongside the romance between Chase and Tavia we get to see a lot more of the other Warriors and their mates. There were some scenes between Lucan and Gabrielle that melted my heart and reminded me just why I love him so much, there was also a conversation with Lucan and Tegan that brought tears to my eyes and I really want to just start reading the whole series again from the beginning. Dragos has some shocking plans that cause complete chaos for all of the warriors and things will never be the same again after this installment. The action was breathtaking and it was impossible to guess what would happen next and the ending actually left me in tears of happiness.<br /><br />I panicked for a few minutes because this book wraps everything up so well that it could easily be the end of the series and I'm really not ready for the series to end! I was happy to confirm that the series will continue but I believe that the focus will now move onto the younger generation of the breed with the next book being Mira's story. Darker After Midnight is an unmissable installment to the series and one I can't recommend highly enough - this book will blow you away! I for one can't wait to see where Lara Adrian takes us next and am already excited about Mira's book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10147027268220914571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oVPf2LGXgERhVhn2rsSsMeJSpWkDVJnd3sBG5PZ3yYLPG07BUDbFD80CC1XbfmlGGaQvC4smptNDCjVyciJebA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer1570874887144392948"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers hav</span>
  <span id="freeText1570874887144392948" style="display:none"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers have called Lara’s books “addictively readable” (Chicago Tribune), “extraordinary” (Fresh Fiction), “strikingly original” (Booklist), and “one of the best vampire series on the market” (Romantic Times).<br /> <br />Writing as <b>TINA ST. JOHN</b>, her historical romances have won numerous awards including the National Readers Choice; Romantic Times Magazine Reviewer’s Choice; Booksellers Best; and many others. She was twice named a Finalist in Romance Writers of America’s RITA Awards, for Best Historical Romance (White Lion’s Lady) and Best Paranormal Romance (Heart of the Hunter). More recently, the German translation of Heart of the Hunter debuted on Der Spiegel bestseller list.<br /><br />With an ancestry stretching back to the Mayflower and the court of King Henry VIII, the author lives with her husband in New England, where she is working on her next novel. Visit Lara’s website and sign up for new release announcements at <a href="http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews" rel="nofollow noopener">http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews</a><br /></span>
